# 0) ê³µí†µ ê·œì•½(Frontend â†” Backend)

## 0.1 ë¦¬ì†ŒìŠ¤ ë„¤ì´ë°

* `ip_listings` (ê³µê¸‰í˜• IP)
* `demand_requests` (ìˆ˜ìš”ìš”ì²­)

* ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸: `{ items: [...], page, page_size, total }`
* ë‹¨ê±´: `{ data: ... }`
* ì—ëŸ¬: `{ error_code, message, fields? }`

## ë‹¤ìŒ(ì¦‰ì‹œ ì´ì–´ì„œ ê°€ëŠ¥)

ì´ì œ FE/BEê°€ ë°”ë¡œ ê°œë°œ ë“¤ì–´ê°€ë ¤ë©´, ë‹¤ìŒ ì¤‘ í•˜ë‚˜ë¡œ í™•ì •í•´ì£¼ë©´ ì¢‹ìŒ(ì§ˆë¬¸ ì—†ì´ ë‚´ê°€ ì´ˆì•ˆ ì‘ì„± ê°€ëŠ¥):

1. **API ìŠ¤í™ì„ OpenAPI(YAML) í˜•íƒœë¡œ ì •ë¦¬**
2. **ê° ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ Request/Response ì˜ˆì‹œ JSONê¹Œì§€ ì‘ì„±**
3. **ìƒíƒœ ì „ì´ ë‹¤ì´ì–´ê·¸ë¨(Room/Document/Offer) ì •ë¦¬**

ì›í•˜ëŠ” ë²ˆí˜¸ ë§í•´ì¤˜.


[ì§ˆë¬¸]
API ìŠ¤í™ì„ OpenAPI(YAML) í˜•íƒœë¡œ ì •ë¦¬í•´ì¤˜.



[ë‹µë³€]
```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: IP Marketplace Platform API
  version: "0.1.0"
  description: >
    MVP ì¤‘ì‹¬ OpenAPI ì´ˆì•ˆ. ê³µê¸‰í˜• IP Listing, ìˆ˜ìš”í˜• Demand Request/Proposal,
    Room(Deal/License/Valuation), Documents/Signature, Messages, Settlement, AuditLog,
    Mandate(ìœ„ì„) í¬í•¨.

servers:
  - url: https://api.example.com
    description: Production
  - url: https://staging-api.example.com
    description: Staging

tags:
  - name: Auth
  - name: IPListings
  - name: DemandRequests
  - name: Proposals
  - name: Rooms
  - name: Offers
  - name: Documents
  - name: Messages
  - name: Settlements
  - name: AuditLogs
  - name: Mandates
  - name: Valuators
  - name: Wallet

security:
  - bearerAuth: []

paths:
  /health:
    get:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Health check
      security: []
      responses:
        "200":
          description: OK

  /me:
    get:
      tags: [Auth]
      summary: Get current user profile
      responses:
        "200":
          description: OK
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: "#/components/schemas/MeResponse"

  /ip_listings:
    get:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Search IP listings
      parameters:
        - in: query
          name: q
          schema: { type: string }
        - in: query
          name: ipc
          description: IPC/CPC codes
          schema:
            type: array
            items: { type: string }
          style: form
          explode: true
        - in: query
          name: industry
          schema:
            type: array
            items: { type: string }
          style: form
          explode: true
        - in: query
          name: ip_type
          schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPType" }
        - in: query
          name: filing_status
          schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/FilingStatus" }
        - in: query
          name: listing_status
          schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ListingStatus" }
        - in: query
          name: license_available
          schema: { type: boolean }
        - in: query
          name: exclusive
          schema: { type: boolean }
        - in: query
          name: region
          schema:
            type: array
            items: { type: string }
          style: form
          explode: true
        - in: query
          name: broker_managed
          schema: { type: boolean }
        - in: query
          name: price_min
          schema: { type: number }
        - in: query
          name: price_max
          schema: { type: number }
        - in: query
          name: sort
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [latest, relevance, price_asc, price_desc, views_desc]
          default: latest
        - in: query
          name: page
          schema: { type: integer, minimum: 1, default: 1 }
        - in: query
          name: page_size
          schema: { type: integer, minimum: 1, maximum: 100, default: 20 }
      responses:
        "200":
          description: OK
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: "#/components/schemas/PaginatedIPListingCard"
    post:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Create IP listing (Owner/Broker with mandate)
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingCreate" }
      responses:
        "201":
          description: Created
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingResponse" }

  /ip_listings/{ip_listing_id}:
    get:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Get IP listing detail
      parameters:
        - $ref: "#/components/parameters/IPListingId"
      responses:
        "200":
          description: OK
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingDetailResponse" }
    patch:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Update IP listing (Owner/Broker with mandate)
      parameters:
        - $ref: "#/components/parameters/IPListingId"
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingUpdate" }
      responses:
        "200":
          description: OK
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingResponse" }

  /ip_listings/{ip_listing_id}/favorites:
    post:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Add favorite
      parameters:
        - $ref: "#/components/parameters/IPListingId"
      responses:
        "204": { description: No Content }
    delete:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Remove favorite
      parameters:
        - $ref: "#/components/parameters/IPListingId"
      responses:
        "204": { description: No Content }

  /ip_listings/{ip_listing_id}/inquiries:
    post:
      tags: [IPListings]
      summary: Create inquiry (may create room)
      parameters:
        - $ref: "#/components/parameters/IPListingId"
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/InquiryCreate" }
      responses:
        "201":
          description: Created
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/InquiryResponse" }

  /demand_requests:
    get:
      tags: [DemandRequests]
      summary: Search demand requests
      parameters:
        - in: query
          name: q
          schema: { type: string }
        - in: query
          name: request_type
          schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/DemandRequestType" }
        - in: query
          name: industry
          schema:
            type: array
            items: { type: string }
          style: form
          explode: true
        - in: query
          name: region
          schema:
            type: array
            items: { type: string }
          style: form
          explode: true
        - in: query
          name: budget_min
          schema: { type: number }
        - in: query
          name: budget_max
          schema: { type: number }
        - in: query
          name: deadline_before
          schema: { type: string, format: date-time }
        - in: query
          name: anonymous
          schema: { type: boolean }
        - in: query
          name: status
          schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/DemandRequestStatus" }
        - in: query
          name: sort
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [latest, deadline_asc, relevance]
          default: latest
        - in: query
          name: page
          schema: { type: integer, minimum: 1, default: 1 }
        - in: query
          name: page_size
          schema: { type: integer, minimum: 1, maximum: 100, default: 20 }
      responses:
        "200":
          description: OK
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/PaginatedDemandRequestCard" }
    post:
      tags: [DemandRequests]
      summary: Create demand request (Buyer)
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/DemandRequestCreate" }
      responses:
        "201":
          description: Created
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/DemandRequestResponse" }

  /demand_requests/{demand_request_id}:
    get:
      tags: [DemandRequests]
      summary: Get demand request detail

components:
  securitySchemes:
    bearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT

  parameters:
    IPListingId:
      in: path
      name: ip_listing_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    DemandRequestId:
      in: path
      name: demand_request_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    ProposalId:
      in: path
      name: proposal_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    RoomId:
      in: path
      name: room_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    OfferId:
      in: path
      name: offer_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    DocumentId:
      in: path
      name: document_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    MandateId:
      in: path
      name: mandate_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
    ValuatorId:
      in: path
      name: valuator_id
      required: true
      schema: { type: string, format: uuid }

  schemas:
    # ---- Enums ----
    UserRole:
      type: string
      enum: [Owner, Buyer, Broker, Valuator, Admin]

    IPType:
      type: string
      enum: [Patent, UtilityModel, Design, Trademark, Copyright, TradeSecret, Other]

    FilingStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Filed, Registered, Lapsed, Pending, Unknown]

    ListingStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Draft, Published, Paused, UnderNegotiation, Sold, Archived]

    DemandRequestType:
      type: string
      enum: [Purchase, License]

    DemandRequestStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Draft, Open, Negotiating, Closed, Expired]

    ProposalStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Draft, Sent, Countered, Accepted, Rejected, Withdrawn]

    RoomType:
      type: string
      enum: [Deal, License, Valuation]

    RoomStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Setup, Negotiating, Signing, Settling, Completed, Terminated]

    OfferType:
      type: string
      enum: [Assignment, License, ValuationScope, Amendment]

    DocumentType:
      type: string
      enum: [NDA, LOI, AssignmentAgreement, LicenseAgreement, Invoice, Receipt, Report, Amendment, Other]

    DocumentStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Draft, Shared, SignRequested, Signed, Rejected, Expired]

    ConfidentialLevel:
      type: string
      enum: [Public, Private, Strict]

    AccessScope:
      type: string
      enum: [RoomParticipants, OwnerOnly, BuyerOnly, BrokerOnly, ValuatorOnly, Custom]

    MandateStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Pending, Active, Suspended, Terminated]

    SettlementStatus:
      type: string
      enum: [Pending, PartiallyPaid, Paid, Refunded, Disputed]

    # ---- Common ----
    MoneyRange:
      type: object
      properties:
        min: { type: number, nullable: true }
        max: { type: number, nullable: true }
        currency: { type: string, example: KRW }

    Pagination:
      type: object
      properties:
        page: { type: integer }
        page_size: { type: integer }
        total: { type: integer }

    PermissionSet:
      type: object
      properties:
        can_edit: { type: boolean }
        can_propose: { type: boolean }
        can_sign: { type: boolean }
        can_view_private_docs: { type: boolean }
        can_manage_settlement: { type: boolean }
        can_terminate_room: { type: boolean }

    FileRef:
      type: object
      properties:
        file_id: { type: string, format: uuid }
        filename: { type: string }
        content_type: { type: string }
        size_bytes: { type: integer }
        download_url: { type: string, format: uri }

    PartyRef:
      type: object
      properties:
        party_id: { type: string, format: uuid }
        display_name: { type: string }
        role: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/UserRole" }
        agent_role:
          type: string
          nullable: true
          enum: [SellerAgent, BuyerAgent, DualAgent]

    # ---- Auth ----
    MeResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        data:
          type: object
          properties:
            user_id: { type: string, format: uuid }
            email: { type: string, format: email }
            roles:
              type: array
              items: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/UserRole" }
            org:
              type: object
              nullable: true
              properties:
                org_id: { type: string, format: uuid }
                name: { type: string }

    # ---- IP Listing ----
    IPListingCard:
      type: object
      properties:
        id: { type: string, format: uuid }
        title: { type: string }
        summary: { type: string }
        ip_type: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPType" }
        country: { type: string, example: KR }
        filing_status: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/FilingStatus" }
        listing_status: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ListingStatus" }
        license_available: { type: boolean }
        broker_managed: { type: boolean }
        price_range: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/MoneyRange" }
        tags:
          type: array
          items: { type: string }
        updated_at: { type: string, format: date-time }

    PaginatedIPListingCard:
      type: object
      properties:
        items:
          type: array
          items: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingCard" }
        page: { type: integer }
        page_size: { type: integer }
        total: { type: integer }

    RightHolderShare:
      type: object
      properties:
        name: { type: string }
        share_percent: { type: number, nullable: true }

    IPListingCreate:
      type: object
      required: [title, ip_type, country]
      properties:
        title: { type: string }
        summary: { type: string }
        ip_type: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPType" }
        country: { type: string }
        filing_status: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/FilingStatus" }
        application_no: { type: string, nullable: true }
        registration_no: { type: string, nullable: true }
        ipc:
          type: array
          items: { type: string }
        industries:
          type: array
          items: { type: string }
        right_holders:
          type: array
          items: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/RightHolderShare" }
        license_available: { type: boolean, default: false }
        listing_status: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ListingStatus" }
        visibility:
          type: string
          enum: [Full, Teaser, Private]
          default: Teaser
        price_range: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/MoneyRange" }

    IPListingUpdate:
      allOf:
        - $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingCreate"

      type: object

          $ref: "#/components/schemas/IPListingCard"

                    agent_role:
                      type: string
                      enum: [SellerAgent, BuyerAgent, DualAgent]

                  type: object
                  nullable: true

                      type: string

                      type: array

                  $ref: "#/components/schemas/PermissionSet"
```

# 1) ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ë³„ Request/Response ì˜ˆì‹œ JSON

## 1. Health / Me

### GET /health (Response 200)

```json
{ "ok": true }
```

### GET /me (Response 200)

```json
{
  "data": {
    "user_id": "c1a9f3a5-7d7d-4f30-b03e-5e6d1c7e2b1a",
    "email": "user@company.com",
    "roles": ["Buyer", "Owner"],
    "org": { "org_id": "8f0f9b3c-4c6b-4d5a-9a10-3c1a6b8f0b21", "name": "ABC Corp" }
  }
}
```

```json
{
  "data": {
    "id": "0f4a0f46-ec3d-4a41-8f04-8a06f9e5cf7e",
    "title": "3D ìœ ë¡œ ê¸°ë°˜ ë‹¤ì¤‘ ë¶„ì„ ì§„ë‹¨ í‚¤íŠ¸",
    "summary": "3D ìœ ì²´ ê²½ë¡œë¥¼ ì´ìš©í•œ ë‹¤ì¤‘ íƒ€ê¹ƒ ê²€ì¶œ",
```

# 2) ìƒíƒœ ì „ì´ ë‹¤ì´ì–´ê·¸ë¨ ì •ë¦¬ (Room / Document / Offer)

ì•„ë˜ëŠ” â€œí…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë‹¤ì´ì–´ê·¸ë¨ + ì „ì´ ì¡°ê±´(Guard)â€ë¡œ ì •ë¦¬í–ˆì–´. ê°œë°œì—ì„œëŠ” ì´ëŒ€ë¡œ **ìƒíƒœ ë¨¸ì‹ **ìœ¼ë¡œ êµ¬í˜„í•˜ë©´ ë¨.

## 2.1 Room ìƒíƒœ ì „ì´

```
Setup
  -> Negotiating
      -> Signing
          -> Settling
              -> Completed
  -> Terminated (ì–¸ì œë“ , ê¶Œí•œì+ì‚¬ìœ )
Negotiating -> Terminated
Signing     -> Terminated (ì„œëª… ê±°ì ˆ/ê¸°í•œë§Œë£Œ/í•©ì˜íŒŒê¸°)
Settling    -> Terminated (ë¶„ìŸìœ¼ë¡œ ì¢…ë£Œ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì„ íƒ ì‹œ)
```

### ì „ì´ íŠ¸ë¦¬ê±°(ì˜ˆ)

* Setup â†’ Negotiating: ì²« Offer/ë¬¸ì„œ ê³µìœ /ë¬¸ì˜ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì™„ë£Œ
* Negotiating â†’ Signing: â€œìµœì¢… ì˜¤í¼ Acceptedâ€ AND â€œê³„ì•½ì„œ ì´ˆì•ˆ(í•„ìˆ˜ ë¬¸ì„œ) ì¤€ë¹„ë¨â€
* Signing â†’ Settling: â€œí•„ìˆ˜ ì„œëª… ë¬¸ì„œ Signedâ€ (ì˜ˆ: NDA í•„ìˆ˜ë©´ NDA+ë³¸ê³„ì•½)
* Settling â†’ Completed: â€œê²°ì œ/ì •ì‚° Paid + Finalizeâ€
* Any â†’ Terminated: `terminate_room` í˜¸ì¶œ(ê¶Œí•œì) ë˜ëŠ” ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ë§Œë£Œ ì •ì±…

### Guard(ì°¨ë‹¨ ê·œì¹™)

* `Signing` ë‹¨ê³„ì—ì„œëŠ” ìƒˆë¡œìš´ Offer ìƒì„± ê¸ˆì§€(ëŒ€ì‹  Amendment ë¬¸ì„œ í”Œë¡œìš°)
* `Completed` ì´í›„ ìˆ˜ì • ë¶ˆê°€(ë¬¸ì„œë§Œ ì•„ì¹´ì´ë¸Œ/ì—´ëŒ)

---

## 2.2 Document ìƒíƒœ ì „ì´

```
Draft
  -> Shared
      -> SignRequested
          -> Signed
          -> Rejected
          -> Expired
Rejected -> Draft (ìƒˆ ë²„ì „ ì—…ë¡œë“œ ë˜ëŠ” Amendment ìƒì„±)
Signed   -> (locked)  [ìƒˆ ë²„ì „ì€ Amendmentë¡œë§Œ]
```

### ì „ì´ íŠ¸ë¦¬ê±°

* Draft â†’ Shared: ì—…ë¡œë“œ ì™„ë£Œ ë˜ëŠ” í…œí”Œë¦¿ ìƒì„± ì™„ë£Œ
* Shared â†’ SignRequested: ì„œëª…ì ì§€ì • + ì„œëª… ìš”ì²­ ë°œì†¡
* SignRequested â†’ Signed: ëª¨ë“  signerê°€ Signed
* SignRequested â†’ Rejected: signer ì¤‘ 1ëª…ì´ë¼ë„ Reject (ì •ì±… ì„ íƒ)
* SignRequested â†’ Expired: deadline ê²½ê³¼

### Guard

* Signed ë¬¸ì„œëŠ” ì‚­ì œ/ìˆ˜ì • ê¸ˆì§€(ì•„ì¹´ì´ë¸Œë§Œ)
* Signed ì´í›„ ì¡°ê±´ ë³€ê²½ í•„ìš” ì‹œ: `DocumentType=Amendment` ìƒˆ ë¬¸ì„œë¡œë§Œ ì²˜ë¦¬

---

## 2.3 Offer ìƒíƒœ ì „ì´ (Room í˜‘ìƒ)

```
Sent
  -> Countered (ìƒëŒ€ê°€ ì¹´ìš´í„° ì œì•ˆ)
  -> Accepted
  -> Rejected
  -> Withdrawn (ì œì•ˆìê°€ ì² íšŒ)
Countered
  -> Accepted
  -> Rejected
  -> Withdrawn
Accepted -> (lock)
Rejected -> (end)
Withdrawn -> (end)
```

### ì „ì´ íŠ¸ë¦¬ê±°/ì •ì±…

* CounteredëŠ” â€œìƒˆ Offerë¥¼ ìƒì„±â€í•˜ëŠ” ë°©ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ êµ¬í˜„í•´ë„ ë¨(ì¶”ì²œ)

  * ì¦‰, ê¸°ì¡´ OfferëŠ” Replaced, ìƒˆ Offerê°€ Sentë¡œ ìƒì„±
* Accepted ë˜ë©´ Roomì˜ `current_terms` ê°±ì‹  + Signing ì¡°ê±´ ì¶©ì¡± ì—¬ë¶€ ì²´í¬

### Guard

* Room ìƒíƒœê°€ Signing/Settling/Completedë©´ Offer ìƒì„± ì°¨ë‹¨
* WithdrawëŠ” ì œì•ˆìë§Œ ê°€ëŠ¥, Accepted ì´í›„ ë¶ˆê°€

---

# 3) ë°±ì—”ë“œ ë‹¨ì—ì„œ ì¶”ê°€ë¡œ ê³ ë ¤/ê³„íší•´ì•¼ í•  ì  (í•µì‹¬ ì²´í¬ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸)

## 3.1 ê¶Œí•œ/ìœ„ì„(RBAC + ABAC) ì„¤ê³„ê°€ â€œì„±íŒ¨â€

* ë‹¨ìˆœ Role ê¸°ë°˜(RBAC)ë§Œìœ¼ë¡œëŠ” ë¶€ì¡±:
  **Mandate(ìœ„ì„) + Scope(í–‰ìœ„ ê¶Œí•œ) + Object(íŠ¹ì • IP/Room ë²”ìœ„)**ê°€ í•„ìš”
* ì‘ë‹µì— `permissions`ë¥¼ í•­ìƒ í¬í•¨(í”„ë¡ íŠ¸ ê°€ë“œ ë‹¨ìˆœí™”)

## 3.2 íŒŒì¼/ë¬¸ì„œ ì €ì¥ ì „ëµ (ê°€ì¥ ë§ì´ í„°ì§)

* **Pre-signed URL ì—…ë¡œë“œ** ê¶Œì¥(ëŒ€ìš©ëŸ‰/ì†ë„/ë¹„ìš©)
* ë¬¸ì„œ ë²„ì „ ì •ì±…:

  * ê°™ì€ ë¬¸ì„œíƒ€ì…ì´ë¼ë„ v1/v2ê°€ ê°€ëŠ¥
  * Signed ì´í›„ì—ëŠ” â€œAmendmentâ€ë¡œë§Œ í™•ì¥
* ì ‘ê·¼ê¶Œí•œ(AccessScope) ê°•ì œ ê²€ì¦:

  * â€œë§í¬ë§Œ ì•Œë©´ ë‹¤ìš´ë¡œë“œâ€ ë°©ì§€(ì„œëª…ëœ URLë„ TTL ì§§ê²Œ)

## 3.3 ê°ì‚¬ë¡œê·¸(Audit)ì™€ ë¶„ìŸ ëŒ€ë¹„ëŠ” â€œí•„ìˆ˜â€

* ì—´ëŒ/ë‹¤ìš´/ì—…ë¡œë“œ/ì„œëª…/ê¶Œí•œë³€ê²½/ì •ì‚° ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ëª¨ë‘ ë¡œê·¸
* ë¡œê·¸ëŠ” **ìˆ˜ì • ë¶ˆê°€(append-only)** ê¶Œì¥

## 1) IA ì¶”ê°€: Broker(ì¤‘ê°œì) ê³µê°œ í”„ë¡œí•„ + ìœ„ì„ ì˜ë¢°

### 1.1 ìƒˆ ë©”ë‰´/í˜ì´ì§€

* **Brokers(ì¤‘ê°œì ì°¾ê¸°)** *(Expertsì™€ ë™ì¼ ë ˆë²¨)*

# 0. Executive Summary

ë³¸ ì‚¬ì—…ì€ **ì§€ì‹ì¬ì‚°ê¶Œ(IP: íŠ¹í—ˆÂ·ë””ìì¸Â·ìƒí‘œ ë“±)**ì„ ë³´ìœ í•œ ê¶Œë¦¬ìì™€ ì´ë¥¼ í•„ìš”ë¡œ í•˜ëŠ” ìˆ˜ìš”ì(êµ¬ë§¤ì)ë¥¼ ì—°ê²°í•˜ì—¬, **ì–‘ë„(ë§¤ê°)Â·ë¼ì´ì„ ìŠ¤(ì‹¤ì‹œê¶Œ)Â·ê°€ì¹˜í‰ê°€(í‰ê°€ì ì—°ê³„)**ë¥¼ í•˜ë‚˜ì˜ íë¦„ìœ¼ë¡œ ì²˜ë¦¬í•˜ëŠ” **B2B IP ê±°ë˜Â·ì¤‘ê°œÂ·ë¬¸ì„œê´€ë¦¬ í†µí•© í”Œë«í¼**ì„ êµ¬ì¶•í•˜ëŠ” ê²ƒì´ë‹¤.

IP ê±°ë˜ëŠ” ì •ë³´ ë¹„ëŒ€ì¹­, ì‹ ë¢° ë¶€ì¡±, ê³„ì•½Â·ì¦ë¹™ì„œë¥˜ì˜ ë³µì¡ì„±ìœ¼ë¡œ ì¸í•´ â€œê²€ìƒ‰ì€ ë˜ì§€ë§Œ ê±°ë˜ëŠ” ì˜ ì•ˆ ë˜ëŠ”â€ êµ¬ì¡°ê°€ ë°˜ë³µëœë‹¤. ì •ë¶€/ê³µê³µì—ì„œë„ IP ê±°ë˜ í”Œë«í¼ê³¼ ì§€ì› ì²´ê³„ë¥¼ ìš´ì˜í•˜ê³  ìˆìœ¼ë‚˜(ì˜ˆ: êµ­ê°€ ì§€ì‹ì¬ì‚° ê±°ë˜ í”Œë«í¼ IP-MARKET ë“±) ([ipmarket.or.kr][1]), ì‹¤ì œ ê±°ë˜ ì„±ì‚¬ì— í•„ìš”í•œ **í˜‘ìƒÂ·ê¶Œí•œ(ìœ„ì„)Â·ë¬¸ì„œ/ì„œëª…Â·ì •ì‚°Â·ê°ì‚¬ë¡œê·¸**ê¹Œì§€ ì¼ê´€ëœ ì‚¬ìš©ì ê²½í—˜ìœ¼ë¡œ í†µí•©í•œ ë¯¼ê°„í˜• ì†”ë£¨ì…˜ì€ ì—¬ì „íˆ ê°œì„  ì—¬ì§€ê°€ í¬ë‹¤.

ìš°ë¦¬ëŠ” ì´ë¥¼ í•´ê²°í•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•´ â€œê±°ë˜ê°€ ì„±ì‚¬ë˜ëŠ” ê³µê°„â€ì¸ **Deal Room**ì„ ì¤‘ì‹¬ìœ¼ë¡œ, ê³µê¸‰í˜• ë“±ë¡(ê¶Œë¦¬ì ë“±ë¡)ê³¼ ìˆ˜ìš”í˜• ë“±ë¡(êµ¬ë§¤ì ìš”êµ¬ ëª…ì„¸)ì„ ë™ì‹œì— ìš´ì˜í•˜ê³ , ì¤‘ê°œì(ê¸°ìˆ ê±°ë˜ì‚¬) ë° í‰ê°€ì(ê°€ì¹˜í‰ê°€ê¸°ê´€)ê°€ ì°¸ì—¬í•˜ëŠ” **ì „ë¬¸ê°€ ë§ˆì¼“**ì„ ê²°í•©í•œë‹¤.

---

# 1. ì‹œì¥ ë° ê¸°íšŒ

## 1.1 ì‹œì¥ ë°°ê²½: ê¸°ìˆ ì´ì „/ê±°ë˜ëŠ” ëŠ˜ê³ , ë””ì§€í„¸ ì „í™˜ì€ ë” í•„ìš”

* ê¸°ìˆ ê±°ë˜Â·ê¸°ìˆ ì´ì „ì€ â€œê¸°ìˆ ì´ ì–‘ë„, ì‹¤ì‹œê¶Œ í—ˆì—¬ ë“±ì„ í†µí•´ ì´ì „ë˜ëŠ” ê²ƒâ€ìœ¼ë¡œ ì •ì˜ë˜ë©°, ì •ì±…ì ìœ¼ë¡œë„ ë§¤ë…„ ì§€í‘œÂ·í†µê³„ê°€ ê´€ë¦¬ë˜ëŠ” ì˜ì—­ì´ë‹¤. ([ì§€í‘œëˆ„ë¦¬][2])
* ê³µê³µì—°êµ¬ê¸°ê´€(ëŒ€í•™Â·ê³µê³µì—°êµ¬ì†Œ ë“±) ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ, 2022ë…„ ê¸°ìˆ ì´ì „ ìˆ˜ì…ì€ **2,810ì–µ ì›**ì´ë©°(ì „ë…„ ëŒ€ë¹„ ì¦ê°€), ê°™ì€ í•´ ê¸°ìˆ ì´ì „ ê±´ìˆ˜ëŠ” **12,057ê±´**ìœ¼ë¡œ ì§‘ê³„ëœë‹¤. ([ì§€í‘œëˆ„ë¦¬][2])
* ì‚°ì—…í†µìƒìì›ë¶€ ë³´ë„ìë£Œì—ì„œë„ **ê¸°ìˆ ì´ì „ ìˆ˜ì… 2,810ì–µ ì›(ì „ë…„ ëŒ€ë¹„ +5.9%)**ì´ ì–¸ê¸‰ë˜ë©°, ê³µê³µê¸°ìˆ ì´ì „ì‚¬ì—…í™” ì‹¤íƒœì¡°ì‚¬ ê²°ê³¼ê°€ ì •ì±…Â·ì‚¬ì—… ì„¤ê³„ì— í™œìš©ëœë‹¤. ([ì •ì±…ë¸Œë¦¬í•‘][3])

> í•´ì„: â€œì‹œì¥ ê·œëª¨â€ëŠ” ì¡´ì¬í•˜ê³  ì„±ì¥ íë¦„ë„ í™•ì¸ë˜ë‚˜, ê±°ë˜ ê³¼ì •ì´ ë³µì¡í•´ **ì‹¤ì œ ì„±ì‚¬ìœ¨ê³¼ ì†Œìš”ì‹œê°„**ì´ ë³‘ëª©ì´ ëœë‹¤. í”Œë«í¼ì€ ê·¸ ë³‘ëª©ì„ ì¤„ì—¬ **ê±°ë˜ ì „í™˜ìœ¨ê³¼ í‰ê·  ê±°ë˜ ë‹¨ê°€**ë¥¼ ê°œì„ í•˜ëŠ” ë°©í–¥ìœ¼ë¡œ ê°€ì¹˜ê°€ ìƒê¸´ë‹¤.

# 5. ë§ˆì¼€íŒ…Â·ì„¸ì¼ì¦ˆ ì „ëµ(GTM)

## 5.2 ì½œë“œìŠ¤íƒ€íŠ¸(ì–‘ë©´ì‹œì¥) í•´ë²•: â€œê±°ë˜ê°€ ë˜ëŠ” ê³µê¸‰â€ì„ ë¨¼ì € ë§Œë“ ë‹¤
